Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle

✅ ❌ 🪓 💼 🗑️
effect

  • If you control a WIND Fairy monster with 0 ATK, you can Special Summon this card (from your hand). You can only Special Summon "Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle" once per turn this way. If a "Sylphale" monster effect is activated, while this card is on the field or in the GY: You can 1 "Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle" from the GY; send 1 "Sylphale" card from your Deck to the GY, then, if this card is on the field, you can make this card gain or lose original 900 DEF. You can only use this effect of "Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle" once per turn.

➡️
effect

  • If you control a WIND Fairy monster with 0 ATK, you can Special Summon this card (from your hand). You can only Special Summon "Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle" once per turn this way. If a "Sylphale" monster effect is activated, while this card is on the field or in the GY: You can banish 1 "Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle" from your GY; send 1 "Sylphale" card from your Deck to the GY, then, if this card is on the field, you can make this card gain or lose original 900 DEF. You can only use this effect of "Sylphale Zephyrus Thistle" once per turn.

Suzerain Goddess of Dawn & Dusk

✅ ❌ 🪓 💼 🗑️
effect

  • "Suzerain Goddess of the Daylight" + "Suzerain Goddess of the Night Sky"
  • This card is treated as a LIGHT and DARK monster while face-up in your possession. If this card battles a monster, neither can be destroyed by that battle. If this card battles an opponent's monster, at the end of the Damage Step: Send that monster to the GY. Unaffected by your opponent's card effects. Once per turn (Quick Effect): You can Tribute this card; Special Summon up to 2 other "Suzerain" monsters from your GY.

➡️
effect

Cybernailation Ritual

✅ ❌ 🪓 💼 🗑️
effect

  • Banish 4 "Cybernailation" Link Monsters with different names from your GY; Special Summon 1 Link-8 "Cybernailation" Link Monster from your Extra Deck. (This is treated as a Link Summon.) You cannot Special Summon monsters from the extra Deck the turn you activate this card, except Link Monsters with an odd Link Rating and "Cybernailation" monsters. You can only activate 1 "Cybernailation Ritual" per turn.

You can only activate 1 "Cybernailation Ritual" per turn.

effect

  • ● If a monster(s) is sent to your opponent's GY: You can add 1 "The Mad Doctor" from your Deck to your hand, or, if that monster(s) was sent there by your card effect, you can Special Summon 1 "The Mad Doctor" from your Deck instead.
  • ●During the Main Phase, if you control a Level 8 or higher Spellcaster monster: You can Tribute 1 Zombie monster; add 1 "Chirurgeon" Spell from your Deck to your hand.

➡️
effect

  • ● If a monster(s) is sent to your opponent's GY: You can add 1 "The Mad Doctor" from your Deck or GY to your hand, or, if that monster(s) was sent there by your card effect, you can Special Summon that "The Mad Doctor" instead.
  • ●During the Main Phase, if you control a Level 8 or higher Spellcaster monster: You can Tribute 1 Zombie monster; add 1 "Chirurgeon" Spell from your Deck to your hand.

✅ ❌ 🪓 💼 🗑️
effect

  • When this card is activated: You can add 1 "Boehstoic Network Fusion" from your Deck or GY to your hand. The first time each "Boehstoic" monster you control would be destroyed by battle each turn, it is not destroyed. "Boehstoic" monsters you control can attack while in face-up Defense Position. If they do, apply their DEF for damage calculation. When a monster your opponent controls declares a direct attack: You can Special Summon 1 "Boehstoic" monster from your Deck in Defense Position. You can only use each effect of "Boehstoic Cityhall" once per turn.

➡️
effect

  • When this card is activated: You can add 1 "Boehstoic Network Fusion" from your Deck or GY to your hand. The first time each "Boehstoic" monster you control would be destroyed by battle each turn, it is not destroyed. "Boehstoic" monsters you control can attack while in face-up Defense Position. If they do, apply their DEF for damage calculation. When a monster your opponent controls declares a direct attack: You can Special Summon 1 "Boehstoic" monster from your Deck in Defense Position, and if you do, change the attack target to that Summoned monster and perform damage calculation. The Summoned monster cannot be destroyed by that battle. You can only use each effect of "Boehstoic Cityhall" once per turn.
